#desc_network_mirror=1. 同路由：回包数据通过交换机直接到达用户(一般是二层环境)。<br>2. 跨路由：回包数据通过网关转发给用户 (一般是三层环境)，转发由静态路由表决定。<br>3. 镜像流量复制：将镜像流量同时复制一份到指定的网卡，接收的网卡可以是多个，<a class="link need-reload" href="{0}">点此查看镜像流量</a>。
desc_network_mirror=1. Same route: The packet return data reaches the user directly through the switch (usually a Layer 2 environment). <br>2. Cross-route: Packet data is forwarded to the user through the gateway (usually a three-tier environment). Forwarding is determined by the static routing table. <br>3. Mirroring traffic replication: copy the mirrored traffic to a specified network card at the same time, and the received network card can be multiple. <a class="link need-reload" href="{0}">Click here to view Mirror traffic</a>.

#avg_load=平均负载
avg_load=Average load
#desc_sys_avg_load=1. 平均负载是衡量系统压力的综合指标，通常大于5表示高负荷，1~5 中等，小于1轻度，正常情况下平均负载应该小于2。<br>2. 磁盘IO是CPU负载中的一部分，如果长期大于30%表示系统对磁盘的读写异常，或磁盘本身有问题。
desc_sys_avg_load=1. Average load is a comprehensive indicator of system pressure. Usually, a load greater than 5 indicates a high load, 1 to 5 medium, or less than 1 light, and an average load under normal conditions should be less than 2. <br>2. Disk IO is a part of the CPU load. If the long term is greater than 30%, it indicates that the system has abnormal read/write operations to the disk, or the disk itself has a problem.

Review function requires hard disk support <span class="need-admin">,<a class="link" href="{0}">Click here to configure storage disk</a></span> . The size of the occupied hard disk depends on the live source stream. Taking 8 Mbps as an example, each channel needs about 80 G per day. <br> 3. The intranet web player only supports H.264+AAC encoding source, it is recommended to use APP or PC player, <a class="link" target="_blank" href="{1}">click to download APP and PC player</a></span>.

#desc_vod_upload_mgr=本地视频功能需要硬盘支持<span class="need-admin">，<a class="link" href="{0}">点此配置存储磁盘</a></span>。轮播数据建议放在根目录之下2级目录，如：<span class="blue">根目录\轮播\轮播1</span>。<span class="hot">轮播仅支持H.264+AAC编码的mp4文件</span>。

#desc_vod_settings=本系统支持通过共享管理本地视频。可以在资源管理器或运行中输入<span class="hot">\\本机IP</span>（如：<span class="hot">\\192.168.1.250</span>），确定然后输入密码进入，<a class="link" href="images/demo/open-share.png" target="_blank">点此查看示例</a>。
desc_vod_settings=This system supports local video management through samba share. You can enter <span class="hot">\\local IP</span> (such as: <span class="hot">\\192.168.1.250</span>) in the resource manager or running, and then Enter the password to enter, <a class="link" href="images/demo/open-share.png" target="_blank">click to view the example</a>.
#desc_vod_list=网页播放器只支持H.264+AAC编码的mp4文件，APP支持大部分常见格式（取决于硬件解码能力），如mp4、mkv、rmvb、avi等。
desc_vod_list=The web player only supports H.264+AAC encoded mp4 files. APP supports most common formats (depending on the hardware decoding capabilities), such as mp4, mkv, rmvb, avi, etc.

#desc_live_user=1. 请先在用户组管理添加用户组并选择对应频道。用户组ID长度为5，如<span class="green">10000</span>；用户ID长度为6，如<span class="color4">100001</span>。<br>2. 使用网络机顶盒看电视时用于登录的用户名为用户组ID和用户ID的组合。例如：用户组ID为<span class="green">10000</span>，用户ID为<span class="color4">100001</span>，那么登录用户名为<span class="green">10000</span><span class="color4">100001</span><br>3. 默认用户账号为（<span class="green">10000</span><span class="color4">100001</span>），若系统检测到默认账号不存在，会自动创建默认账号。若不想启用该账号，您可以禁用该账号。
desc_live_user=1. Please add user groups and select the corresponding channel. The user group ID length is 5, such as <span class="green">10000</span>; the user ID length is 6, such as <span class="color4">100001</span>. <br>2. APP login name equals user group ID + user ID. For example: if the user group ID is <span class="green">10000</span> and the user ID is <span class="color4">100001</span>, the login user name is <span class="green"> 10000</span><span class="color4">100001</span><br>3. The default user account is (<span class="green">10000</span><span class="color4">100001 </span>) If the system detects that the default account does not exist, it will automatically create a default account. If you do not want to enable this account, you can disable it.
